```
Apk:org.yausername.dvd_10301.apk
Err: Found: Untrused PRNG (java.util.Random) in <kotlin.random.FallbackThreadLocalRandom$implStorage$1: java.util.Random initialValue()>::initialValue.

Misuse Num:486
```

ITP: This is just the mapping of Java's util.random to Koitlin's, inside the koitlin-stdlib. See the [source](https://github.com/JetBrains/kotlin/blob/master/libraries/stdlib/jvm/src/kotlin/random/PlatformRandom.kt) here. Because of this, all apps that include the koitlin-stdlib will have a "misuse".

------------------------------------------------
```
#3
Class: androidx.activity.result.ActivityResultRegistry
Method: void <init>()
Apk Num:473

Apk:com.kpstv.xclipper_11.apk
Err: Found: Untrused PRNG (java.util.Random) in <androidx.activity.result.ActivityResultRegistry: void <init>()>::init.

Apk:com.joshuacerdenia.android.nicefeed_18.apk
Err: Found: Untrused PRNG (java.util.Random) in <androidx.activity.result.ActivityResultRegistry: void <init>()>::init.

Apk:io.github.domi04151309.home_180.apk
Err: Found: Untrused PRNG (java.util.Random) in <androidx.activity.result.ActivityResultRegistry: void <init>()>::init.

Misuse Num:473
```

ITP: As can be seen in [the code here](https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+/f2e05c341382db64d127118a13451dcaa554b702/activity/activity/src/main/java/androidx/activity/result/ActivityResultRegistry.java), the `random` is used to generate a register code for the call. The code checks if a generated register code has already been used (and generate a new one if necessary). Moreover, according to [the code here](https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/support/+/refs/heads/androidx-master-dev/activity/activity/src/main/java/androidx/activity/ComponentActivity.java#172), each `ComponentActivity` class has its own `ActivityResultRegistry`, which inherently has some degree of isolation that it's not even like one malicious activity can predict the register code and intercept values that is not meant for it. It's difficult to see how this leads to meaningful attacks.
